\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07182}07182       \textcolor{comment}{/* copy the sample from the circular buffer to the destination buffer */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07183}07183       *dst = circBuffer[rOffset];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07184}07184 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07185}07185       \textcolor{comment}{/* Update the input pointer */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07186}07186       dst += dstInc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07187}07187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07188}07188       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dst == dst\_end)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07189}07189       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07190}07190         dst = dst\_base;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07191}07191       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07192}07192 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07193}07193       \textcolor{comment}{/* Circularly update rOffset.  Watch out for positive and negative value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07194}07194       rOffset += bufferInc;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07195}07195 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07196}07196       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rOffset >= L)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07197}07197       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07198}07198         rOffset -\/= L;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07199}07199       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07200}07200 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07201}07201       \textcolor{comment}{/* Decrement the loop counter */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07202}07202       i-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07203}07203     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07204}07204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07205}07205     \textcolor{comment}{/* Update the index pointer */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07206}07206     *readOffset = rOffset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07207}07207   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l07208}07208 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08725}08725     \textcolor{comment}{/* x1 is in 1.15(q15), xfract in 12.20 format and out is in 13.35 format */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08726}08726     \textcolor{comment}{/* convert 13.35 to 13.31 by right shifting  and out is in 1.31 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08727}08727     out = (q31\_t) (((q63\_t) x1 * (0x0FFFFF -\/ xfract)) >> 4U);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08729}08729 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08730}08730     \textcolor{comment}{/* x2 * (xfract) * (1-\/yfract)  in 1.51 and adding to acc */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{arm__math_8h_source_l08731}08731     out = (q31\_t) (((q63\_t) x2 * (0x0FFFFF -\/ yfract)) >> 4U);}
